  "content": "# Apache Kafka KafkaConsumer Java API Reference\n\n## Table of Contents\n\n1. [Overview](#overview)\n2. [Threading Model](#threading-model)\n3. [Core Types](#core-types)\n4. [Subscription and Assignment](#subscription-and-assignment)\n5. [Polling and Data Fetching](#polling-and-data-fetching)\n6. [Offset Management](#offset-management)\n7. [Flow Control and Position Queries](#flow-control-and-position-queries)\n8. [Consumer Group Mechanics](#consumer-group-mechanics)\n9. [Rebalancing and Callbacks](#rebalancing-and-callbacks)\n10. [Metadata and Monitoring](#metadata-and-monitoring)\n11. [Lifecycle and Resource Management](#lifecycle-and-resource-management)\n12. [Exception Handling](#exception-handling)\n13. [Configuration-Driven Behaviors](#configuration-driven-behaviors)\n14. [Common Patterns and Best Practices](#common-patterns-and-best-practices)\n15. [Usage Examples](#usage-examples)\n\n---\n\n## Overview\n\nThe `KafkaConsumer<K, V>` is a Java client for consuming records from Apache Kafka clusters. It provides a flexible API supporting multiple consumption patterns:\n\n- **Group-managed consumption**: Multiple consumer instances automatically partition work through group coordination\n- **Standalone consumption**: Manual partition assignment for independent consumers\n- **Dynamic topic subscription**: Subscribe to topics and automatically discover new partitions\n- **Manual offset management**: Either automatic or explicit offset commits\n\n### Key Characteristics\n\n- **Not thread-safe**: The consumer instance itself must be confined to a single thread. Only `wakeup()` is thread-safe.\n- **Event loop model**: The consumer processes rebalances and manages group membership only during `poll()` calls\n- **Transparent broker failure handling**: Automatically reconnects to available brokers\n- **Offset semantics**: Provides fine-grained control over consumption position\n\n---\n\n## Threading Model\n\n### Single-Threaded Design\n\nThe `KafkaConsumer` is **not thread-safe** by design. All operations except `wakeup()` must be called from a single consumer thread:\n\n```java\n// \u274c INCORRECT: Multiple threads accessing same consumer\nnew Thread(() -> consumer.poll(Duration.ofSeconds(1))).start();\nnew Thread(() -> consumer.commitSync()).start();\n\n// \u2705 CORRECT: Single-threaded access\nconsumer.poll(Duration.ofSeconds(1));\nconsumer.commitSync();\n```\n\nUnsynchronized multi-threaded access results in `ConcurrentModificationException`.\n\n### Wakeup Exception\n\nThe only thread-safe method is `wakeup()`, which can be called from any thread to interrupt a blocking operation:\n\n```java\n// From separate thread\nconsumer.wakeup();\n```\n\nThis causes any blocking `poll()`, `commitSync()`, or other operation to throw `WakeupException` immediately.\n\n### Pattern: Consumer Thread with Shutdown\n\n```java\npublic class ConsumerRunner implements Runnable {\n    private final AtomicBoolean closed = new AtomicBoolean(false);\n    private final KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer;\n\n    public ConsumerRunner(KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer) {\n        this.consumer = consumer;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void run() {\n        try {\n            consumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic\"));\n            while (!closed.get()) {\n                ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(10000));\n                for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n                    processRecord(record);\n                }\n            }\n        } catch (WakeupException e) {\n            if (!closed.get()) throw e;\n        } finally {\n            consumer.close();\n        }\n    }\n\n    public void shutdown() {\n        closed.set(true);\n        consumer.wakeup();\n    }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Core Types\n\n### KafkaConsumer<K, V>\n\nMain consumer class implementing the `Consumer<K, V>` interface.\n\n#### Constructors\n\n```java\n// Configuration via Map\nKafkaConsumer(Map<String, Object> configs)\nKafkaConsumer(Map<String, Object> configs,\n              Deserializer<K> keyDeserializer,\n              Deserializer<V> valueDeserializer)\n\n// Configuration via Properties\nKafkaConsumer(Properties properties)\nKafkaConsumer(Properties properties,\n              Deserializer<K> keyDeserializer,\n              Deserializer<V> valueDeserializer)\n```\n\n**Note**: Always call `close()` after use to avoid resource leaks (TCP connections, memory buffers).\n\n### ConsumerRecord<K, V>\n\nRepresents a single message fetched from Kafka.\n\n#### Key Fields\n\n```java\nString topic()                      // Topic name\nint partition()                     // Partition ID\nlong offset()                       // Offset in partition\nK key()                            // Message key (may be null)\nV value()                          // Message value\nlong timestamp()                   // Message timestamp\nTimestampType timestampType()      // Timestamp type\nOptional<Integer> leaderEpoch()   // Leader epoch of record\nint serializedKeySize()            // Size of serialized key\nint serializedValueSize()          // Size of serialized value\nHeaders headers()                  // Record headers\nOptional<Short> deliveryCount()   // Delivery count (if available)\n```\n\n**Thread Safety Note**: `ConsumerRecord` is not thread-safe. Concurrent access to a record or its headers may result in `ConcurrentModificationException` or data corruption.\n\n### ConsumerRecords<K, V>\n\nBatch container for records returned from `poll()`.\n\n#### Methods\n\n```java\nList<ConsumerRecord<K, V>> records(TopicPartition partition)\nIterable<ConsumerRecord<K, V>> records(String topic)\nSet<TopicPartition> partitions()\nMap<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> nextOffsets()\nIterator<ConsumerRecord<K, V>> iterator()\nint count()\nboolean isEmpty()\n```\n\n**Critical Semantic**: `nextOffsets()` returns the offset that should be committed for each partition, accounting for all records returned in this batch.\n\n### OffsetAndMetadata\n\nCombines an offset with optional leader epoch and metadata.\n\n```java\npublic class OffsetAndMetadata {\n    long offset()                       // The offset to commit\n    String metadata()                   // Optional metadata string\n    Optional<Integer> leaderEpoch()    // Optional leader epoch\n}\n```\n\n**Semantics**: The offset should represent the **next offset to consume**, not the last consumed offset. For example, if you just processed offset 42, commit 43.\n\n### ConsumerRebalanceListener\n\nCallback interface for partition assignment changes.\n\n```java\npublic interface ConsumerRebalanceListener {\n    void onPartitionsRevoked(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)\n    void onPartitionsAssigned(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)\n    default void onPartitionsLost(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)\n}\n```\n\n**Execution Context**: Callbacks execute synchronously within `poll()` calls, in the consumer thread.\n\n### OffsetCommitCallback\n\nAsynchronous callback for offset commit completion.\n\n```java\n@FunctionalInterface\npublic interface OffsetCommitCallback {\n    void onComplete(Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets,\n                    Exception exception);\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Subscription and Assignment\n\n### Concepts\n\nKafka offers two exclusive modes for determining which partitions to consume:\n\n1. **Topic Subscription** (Group Management): Consumer joins a group, coordinator assigns partitions\n2. **Manual Assignment** (Standalone): Consumer directly owns specific partitions, no group coordination\n\n**Mutually Exclusive**: Cannot mix `subscribe()` and `assign()` without calling `unsubscribe()` first.\n\n### Topic Subscription (Group Management)\n\n#### Subscribe to Specific Topics\n\n```java\nvoid subscribe(Collection<String> topics)\nvoid subscribe(Collection<String> topics, ConsumerRebalanceListener listener)\n```\n\n**Behavior**:\n- Triggers group coordination; consumer joins the group\n- Partitions are assigned by the group coordinator using a `ConsumerPartitionAssignor`\n- Assignment changes automatically when:\n  - Group membership changes (new/failed consumers)\n  - New partitions are added to subscribed topics\n  - Topic metadata changes\n- Rebalances are detected and executed only during `poll()` calls\n- Non-incremental: Calling again replaces the previous subscription\n\n**Example**:\n\n```java\nconsumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic1\", \"topic2\"), new ConsumerRebalanceListener() {\n    @Override\n    public void onPartitionsRevoked(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n        consumer.commitSync();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void onPartitionsAssigned(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n        // Initialize per-partition state\n    }\n});\n```\n\n#### Subscribe via Pattern\n\n```java\nvoid subscribe(Pattern pattern)\nvoid subscribe(Pattern pattern, ConsumerRebalanceListener listener)\nvoid subscribe(SubscriptionPattern pattern)\nvoid subscribe(SubscriptionPattern pattern, ConsumerRebalanceListener listener)\n```\n\n**Behavior**:\n- Periodically checks broker metadata against pattern\n- Automatically includes new matching topics\n- Frequency controlled by `metadata.max.age.ms`\n\n**Example**:\n\n```java\n// Match any topic starting with \"events_\"\nconsumer.subscribe(Pattern.compile(\"events_.*\"));\n```\n\n#### Unsubscribe\n\n```java\nvoid unsubscribe()\n```\n\nClears both topic subscriptions and manual assignments. Returns consumer to \"no subscription\" state.\n\n### Manual Partition Assignment\n\n```java\nvoid assign(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)\n```\n\n**Characteristics**:\n- Disables group coordination entirely\n- No rebalancing; partitions only change via explicit `assign()` calls\n- Consumer acts independently\n- Still uses `group.id` for offset storage, but not for coordination\n- Suitable for standalone consumers or externally-coordinated systems\n\n**Example**:\n\n```java\nTopicPartition partition0 = new TopicPartition(\"topic\", 0);\nTopicPartition partition1 = new TopicPartition(\"topic\", 1);\nconsumer.assign(Arrays.asList(partition0, partition1));\n```\n\n**Use Cases**:\n- State machines with local state per partition\n- External orchestration (e.g., YARN, Kubernetes)\n- Distributed stream processing frameworks\n- Partition-level failure recovery\n\n---\n\n## Polling and Data Fetching\n\n### Poll Semantics\n\n```java\nConsumerRecords<K, V> poll(Duration timeout)\n```\n\n**Critical Behavior**:\n\n1. **Immediate Return**: If records are available or position advances past control/aborted records, returns immediately\n2. **Blocking Wait**: Otherwise waits up to `timeout` for data\n3. **May Block Longer**: Poll can block longer than `timeout` during:\n   - Group rebalances (running `ConsumerRebalanceListener` callbacks)\n   - Metadata refresh\n   - Fetching stable offsets\n4. **Rebalance Execution**: Only during `poll()` are rebalances detected and executed\n5. **Position Advancement**: Automatically updates consumer position as records are returned\n\n**Implementation Pattern**:\n\n```java\nwhile (true) {\n    ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n    for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n        processRecord(record);\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### Offset Behavior During Poll\n\n**Initial State**: Consumer position initialized from one of:\n1. `seek()` calls\n2. Committed offset from `committed()`\n3. Offset reset policy (`auto.offset.reset`)\n\n**Position Tracking**:\n- Position advances **after** records are returned to application\n- Returned records: offsets [position, position + count)\n- After poll returns, position = position + count\n\n**Example**:\n\n```\nInitial position: 100\nPoll returns records with offsets: 100, 101, 102\nNew position: 103\nNext poll returns: 103+\n```\n\n### Empty Records\n\nIf no data is available within the timeout:\n\n```java\nConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\nassert records.isEmpty(); // true\n```\n\n---\n\n## Offset Management\n\n### Offset Concepts\n\n**Position**: Offset of the next record to be fetched. Automatically maintained and advanced by `poll()`.\n\n**Committed Offset**: Last offset whose processing is complete. Used to resume consumption on failure/restart.\n\n**Offset Semantics**: The committed offset should represent the **next offset to consume**, not the last consumed offset.\n\nExample:\n```\nConsumed: [0, 1, 2, 3]\nPosition: 4\nCommit: 4  (not 3!)\n```\n\n### Automatic Offset Commits\n\nWhen `enable.auto.commit=true`:\n\n- Commits offsets periodically (controlled by `auto.commit.interval.ms`)\n- Commit happens asynchronously during `poll()`\n- Commits the current position for all assigned partitions\n\n**Risk**: If application crashes between `poll()` returning records and those records being processed, committed offset may be ahead of actual processing.\n\n```java\n// \u274c RISKY: Auto-commit with sync processing\nconsumer.poll(...);  // Offsets committed after this\n// ... if we crash here, records are lost\nprocessRecords();\n```\n\n### Manual Offset Commits (Synchronous)\n\n```java\nvoid commitSync()                                    // All assigned partitions\nvoid commitSync(Duration timeout)\nvoid commitSync(Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets)\nvoid commitSync(Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets, Duration timeout)\n```\n\n**Behavior**:\n- Blocks until commit succeeds or fails\n- Commits offsets to Kafka's `__consumer_offsets` topic\n- Uses `default.api.timeout.ms` as default timeout\n- Subsequent async commits guaranteed to complete before `commitSync()` returns\n\n**Exceptions**:\n- `CommitFailedException`: Unrecoverable; consumer lost partitions during rebalance\n- `RebalanceInProgressException`: Transient; retry after `poll()`\n- `WakeupException`: `wakeup()` called from another thread\n- `TimeoutException`: Timeout expired\n\n**Pattern: Commit After Processing**\n\n```java\nconsumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic\"));\nwhile (true) {\n    ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n    for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n        processRecord(record);\n    }\n    consumer.commitSync();  // Commit when batch is done\n}\n```\n\n**Pattern: Per-Partition Commits**\n\n```java\nwhile (true) {\n    ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n    for (TopicPartition partition : records.partitions()) {\n        List<ConsumerRecord<String, String>> partitionRecords = records.records(partition);\n        for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : partitionRecords) {\n            processRecord(record);\n        }\n        // Commit just this partition\n        consumer.commitSync(Collections.singletonMap(\n            partition,\n            records.nextOffsets().get(partition)\n        ));\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### Manual Offset Commits (Asynchronous)\n\n```java\nvoid commitAsync()\nvoid commitAsync(OffsetCommitCallback callback)\nvoid commitAsync(Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets, OffsetCommitCallback callback)\n```\n\n**Behavior**:\n- Returns immediately (non-blocking)\n- Sends commit request to broker asynchronously\n- Callback invoked when broker responds\n- Multiple async commits maintain order; callbacks invoked in order\n- Async commits guaranteed to complete before subsequent `commitSync()`\n\n**Callback Semantics**:\n\n```java\nnew OffsetCommitCallback() {\n    @Override\n    public void onComplete(Map<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> offsets,\n                          Exception exception) {\n        if (exception == null) {\n            // Commit succeeded\n        } else {\n            // Commit failed; decide whether to retry or log\n            if (exception instanceof RetriableCommitFailedException) {\n                // Can retry\n            } else if (exception instanceof CommitFailedException) {\n                // Unrecoverable; lost partitions\n            }\n        }\n    }\n};\n```\n\n**Pattern: Async Commits with Buffering**\n\n```java\nconsumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic\"));\nList<ConsumerRecord<String, String>> buffer = new ArrayList<>();\nint batchSize = 1000;\n\nwhile (true) {\n    ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n    for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n        buffer.add(record);\n    }\n\n    if (buffer.size() >= batchSize) {\n        processAndCommit(buffer);\n        buffer.clear();\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### Querying Committed Offsets\n\n```java\nMap<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> committed(Set<TopicPartition> partitions)\nMap<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> committed(Set<TopicPartition> partitions, Duration timeout)\n```\n\n**Behavior**:\n- Fetches last committed offset from broker (blocks)\n- Returns map with `null` value for partitions with no prior commit\n\n**Example**:\n\n```java\nSet<TopicPartition> partitions = consumer.assignment();\nMap<TopicPartition, OffsetAndMetadata> committed = consumer.committed(partitions);\n\nfor (TopicPartition partition : partitions) {\n    OffsetAndMetadata metadata = committed.get(partition);\n    if (metadata != null) {\n        System.out.println(\"Partition \" + partition + \" last committed: \" +\n                          metadata.offset());\n    } else {\n        System.out.println(\"Partition \" + partition + \" never committed\");\n    }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Flow Control and Position Queries\n\n### Pause and Resume\n\n```java\nvoid pause(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)\nvoid resume(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)\nSet<TopicPartition> paused()\n```\n\n**Behavior**:\n- `pause()`: Stops fetching from specified partitions; `poll()` won't return records\n- `resume()`: Resumes fetching from paused partitions\n- Pause state is **not preserved** across rebalances\n- Does not affect subscription\n\n**Use Case: Flow Control**\n\n```java\n// Pause fast partition to let slow partition catch up\nconsumer.pause(Collections.singleton(fastPartition));\n\n// Catch up...\nConsumerRecords<String, String> records;\nwhile (consumer.position(slowPartition) < targetOffset) {\n    records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n    processRecords(records);\n}\n\n// Resume\nconsumer.resume(Collections.singleton(fastPartition));\n```\n\n### Position Queries\n\n```java\nlong position(TopicPartition partition)\nlong position(TopicPartition partition, Duration timeout)\n```\n\n**Semantics**: Returns the offset of the **next record** to be fetched.\n\n**Blocking**: May issue a remote call if position not yet determined (e.g., after assignment).\n\n**Example**:\n\n```\npoll() returned records with offsets [100, 101, 102]\nposition() now returns 103\n```\n\n### Seek Operations\n\n```java\nvoid seek(TopicPartition partition, long offset)\nvoid seek(TopicPartition partition, OffsetAndMetadata offsetAndMetadata)\n```\n\n**Behavior**:\n- Overrides next fetch position\n- Takes effect on next `poll()`\n- Invalid offsets cause `OffsetOutOfRangeException` (depending on `auto.offset.reset`)\n\n**Exception Handling**:\n\n```java\nconsumer.seek(partition, invalidOffset);  // No error yet\nconsumer.poll(Duration.ofSeconds(1));     // OffsetOutOfRangeException now!\n```\n\n### Seek to Boundaries\n\n```java\nvoid seekToBeginning(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)\nvoid seekToEnd(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)\n```\n\n**Semantics**:\n- Lazy evaluation; position set on next `poll()` or `position()` call\n- If collection is empty, applies to all assigned partitions\n- For `seekToEnd()` with `isolation.level=read_committed`:\n  - Seeks to Last Stable Offset (LSO), not absolute end\n  - LSO = min(high watermark, first offset of open transaction)\n\n**Example**:\n\n```java\n// Skip to end of all assigned partitions\nconsumer.seekToEnd(consumer.assignment());\n\n// Process only new messages\nwhile (true) {\n    ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofSeconds(1));\n    for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n        System.out.println(record.value());\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### Offset-to-Timestamp Lookup\n\n```java\nMap<TopicPartition, OffsetAndTimestamp> offsetsForTimes(\n    Map<TopicPartition, Long> timestampsToSearch)\nMap<TopicPartition, OffsetAndTimestamp> offsetsForTimes(\n    Map<TopicPartition, Long> timestampsToSearch, Duration timeout)\n```\n\n**Behavior**:\n- Finds earliest offset with timestamp >= search timestamp\n- Returns `null` if message format version < 0.10.0 (no timestamps)\n- Blocking call; does not require partition assignment\n\n**Example**:\n\n```java\n// Find offset for 1 hour ago\nlong oneHourAgo = System.currentTimeMillis() - (60 * 60 * 1000);\nMap<TopicPartition, Long> timestamps = new HashMap<>();\nfor (TopicPartition partition : consumer.assignment()) {\n    timestamps.put(partition, oneHourAgo);\n}\n\nMap<TopicPartition, OffsetAndTimestamp> offsetsByTime = consumer.offsetsForTimes(timestamps);\n\nfor (TopicPartition partition : consumer.assignment()) {\n    OffsetAndTimestamp offsetAndTimestamp = offsetsByTime.get(partition);\n    if (offsetAndTimestamp != null) {\n        consumer.seek(partition, offsetAndTimestamp.offset());\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### Beginning and End Offsets\n\n```java\nMap<TopicPartition, Long> beginningOffsets(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)\nMap<TopicPartition, Long> beginningOffsets(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions, Duration timeout)\nMap<TopicPartition, Long> endOffsets(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions)\nMap<TopicPartition, Long> endOffsets(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions, Duration timeout)\n```\n\n**Semantics**:\n- Query only; do not change position\n- `beginningOffsets()`: First offset in partition\n- `endOffsets()` in `read_uncommitted`: High watermark (last replicated offset + 1)\n- `endOffsets()` in `read_committed`: Last Stable Offset (first open transaction)\n- Returns empty map if zero timeout provided\n\n**Example**:\n\n```java\nMap<TopicPartition, Long> beginning = consumer.beginningOffsets(consumer.assignment());\nMap<TopicPartition, Long> end = consumer.endOffsets(consumer.assignment());\n\nfor (TopicPartition partition : consumer.assignment()) {\n    long lag = end.get(partition) - consumer.position(partition);\n    System.out.println(\"Partition \" + partition + \" lag: \" + lag);\n}\n```\n\n### Current Lag\n\n```java\nOptionalLong currentLag(TopicPartition topicPartition)\n```\n\n**Behavior**:\n- Returns `OptionalLong.empty()` if lag unknown\n- Uses locally cached metadata\n- May trigger async fetch of log end offset\n\n**Example**:\n\n```java\nfor (TopicPartition partition : consumer.assignment()) {\n    OptionalLong lag = consumer.currentLag(partition);\n    if (lag.isPresent()) {\n        System.out.println(\"Lag: \" + lag.getAsLong());\n    } else {\n        System.out.println(\"Lag unknown\");\n    }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Consumer Group Mechanics\n\n### Group Membership\n\n**Automatic**: When using `subscribe()`, consumer automatically joins group when first `poll()` is called.\n\n**Heartbeats**: Consumer sends periodic heartbeats to coordinator to signal liveness.\n\n**Session Timeout**: If heartbeats not received for `session.timeout.ms`, broker considers consumer dead:\n- Triggers rebalance\n- Partitions reassigned to healthy consumers\n- Consumer that timed out may not know it's been evicted\n\n### Liveness Detection: Max Poll Interval\n\n**Problem**: Heartbeats only prove network connectivity, not processing progress.\n\n**Solution**: `max.poll.interval.ms` - if consumer doesn't call `poll()` frequently enough, it's considered hung:\n\n```java\n// If gap between polls exceeds max.poll.interval.ms...\nsleep(max_poll_interval_ms + 1000);\nconsumer.poll(Duration.ofSeconds(1));  // CommitFailedException!\n```\n\n**Behavior**:\n- Consumer proactively leaves group to allow partition reassignment\n- Any subsequent `commitSync()` fails with `CommitFailedException`\n- Application must call `poll()` to rejoin group\n\n**Tuning**:\n- Increase `max.poll.interval.ms` for slow processing\n- Reduce `max.poll.records` to return fewer records per poll\n- Move processing to separate thread (see patterns below)\n\n### Static Group Membership\n\n**Feature**: Static group instance IDs allow consumers to rejoin without triggering rebalance.\n\n**Configuration**:\n\n```properties\ngroup.instance.id=consumer-1\n```\n\n**Benefit**: Rebalance doesn't occur when consumer restarts if shutdown is brief.\n\n### Group Metadata\n\n```java\nConsumerGroupMetadata groupMetadata()\n```\n\nReturns metadata about consumer's group membership (generational ID, member ID, etc.).\n\n---\n\n## Rebalancing and Callbacks\n\n### Rebalance Triggers\n\nRebalances occur when:\n\n1. **Group membership changes**: Consumer joins/leaves/fails\n2. **Topic subscription changes**: Via `subscribe()` call\n3. **Pattern matches new topics**: Via pattern matching\n4. **Partition count increases**: New partitions added to subscribed topic\n5. **Manual enforcement**: `enforceRebalance()` called\n\n### Rebalance Timeline\n\n1. **Detection**: Broker detects group change\n2. **Initiation**: During `poll()`, consumer receives revoke signal\n3. **Callback - onPartitionsRevoked()**: Application commits offsets, cleans up state\n4. **Partition Assignment**: Assignor runs; partitions reassigned\n5. **Callback - onPartitionsAssigned()**: Application initializes state for new partitions\n6. **Resume Fetching**: `poll()` returns normally\n\n### Callback Ordering\n\n**Standard Path** (eager rebalancing):\n1. `onPartitionsRevoked()` called with all assigned partitions\n2. Rebalance completes\n3. `onPartitionsAssigned()` called with all assigned partitions (even if same)\n\n**Cooperative Rebalancing**:\n1. `onPartitionsRevoked()` called only with partitions actually revoked\n2. Rebalance completes\n3. `onPartitionsAssigned()` called only with new partitions\n\n**Exception Path** (session timeout):\n1. `onPartitionsLost()` called instead of `onPartitionsRevoked()`\n2. Cannot safely commit offsets (partitions already owned by others)\n\n### ConsumerRebalanceListener Implementation\n\n```java\nclass SaveOffsetsOnRebalance implements ConsumerRebalanceListener {\n    private final Consumer<?, ?> consumer;\n    private final OffsetStore store;\n\n    SaveOffsetsOnRebalance(Consumer<?, ?> consumer, OffsetStore store) {\n        this.consumer = consumer;\n        this.store = store;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void onPartitionsRevoked(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n        // Commit offsets before losing partitions\n        for (TopicPartition partition : partitions) {\n            long offset = consumer.position(partition);\n            store.saveOffset(partition, offset);\n        }\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void onPartitionsAssigned(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n        // Restore offsets for new partitions\n        for (TopicPartition partition : partitions) {\n            long offset = store.loadOffset(partition);\n            consumer.seek(partition, offset);\n        }\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void onPartitionsLost(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n        // Partitions already lost; don't try to commit\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### Enforce Rebalance\n\n```java\nvoid enforceRebalance()\nvoid enforceRebalance(String reason)\n```\n\nForces consumer to rejoin group on next `poll()`, triggering rebalance.\n\n**Use Case**: Application state changes warrant partition reassignment based on `ConsumerPartitionAssignor` user data.\n\n---\n\n## Metadata and Monitoring\n\n### Partition Information\n\n```java\nList<PartitionInfo> partitionsFor(String topic)\nList<PartitionInfo> partitionsFor(String topic, Duration timeout)\nMap<String, List<PartitionInfo>> listTopics()\nMap<String, List<PartitionInfo>> listTopics(Duration timeout)\n```\n\n**Behavior**:\n- Fetches metadata from broker (blocking)\n- Does not require assignment or subscription\n- Useful for discovering available topics/partitions\n\n### Metrics\n\n```java\nMap<MetricName, ? extends Metric> metrics()\n```\n\nReturns JMX metrics exposed by consumer. Common metrics:\n\n- `records-consumed-total`: Total records consumed\n- `records-lag-max`: Maximum lag across partitions\n- `fetch-latency-avg`: Average fetch latency\n- `commit-latency-avg`: Average commit latency\n\n### Client Instance ID\n\n```java\nUuid clientInstanceId(Duration timeout)\n```\n\nReturns unique ID for this consumer instance, used in client telemetry. Requires `enable.metrics.push=true`.\n\n---\n\n## Lifecycle and Resource Management\n\n### Creation\n\n```java\n// Via Properties\nProperties props = new Properties();\nprops.setProperty(\"bootstrap.servers\", \"localhost:9092\");\nprops.setProperty(\"group.id\", \"my-group\");\nprops.setProperty(\"key.deserializer\", StringDeserializer.class.getName());\nprops.setProperty(\"value.deserializer\", StringDeserializer.class.getName());\nKafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props);\n\n// Via Map with explicit deserializers\nMap<String, Object> configs = new HashMap<>();\nconfigs.put(\"bootstrap.servers\", \"localhost:9092\");\nconfigs.put(\"group.id\", \"my-group\");\nKafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(\n    configs,\n    new StringDeserializer(),\n    new StringDeserializer()\n);\n```\n\n**Resource Allocation**:\n- TCP connections to brokers\n- Memory buffers for fetching\n- Background thread for metadata updates\n- Group coordination resources\n\n### Closing\n\n```java\nvoid close()                                  // 30-second default timeout, DEFAULT behavior\nvoid close(Duration timeout)                  // Custom timeout (deprecated)\nvoid close(CloseOptions option)              // Timeout + leave group behavior\n```\n\n**close()** does the following:\n\n1. Commits pending offsets (if `enable.auto.commit=true`)\n2. Leaves consumer group (allowing quick rebalance)\n3. Revokes all partitions, triggering `onPartitionsRevoked()`\n4. Closes broker connections\n5. Releases all resources\n\n**CloseOptions**:\n\n```java\nclose(new CloseOptions()\n    .timeout(Duration.ofSeconds(60))\n    .leaveGroup())           // Gracefully leave group\n\nclose(new CloseOptions()\n    .timeout(Duration.ofSeconds(0))\n    .leaveGroup())           // Force close immediately\n```\n\n**Pattern: Try-with-Resources**\n\n```java\ntry (KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props)) {\n    consumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic\"));\n    while (true) {\n        ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofSeconds(1));\n        for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n            processRecord(record);\n        }\n    }\n}  // close() called automatically\n```\n\n---\n\n## Exception Handling\n\n### CommitFailedException\n\n**When**: Synchronous commit fails because consumer lost partitions during rebalance.\n\n**Cause**: `max.poll.interval.ms` exceeded; consumer proactively left group.\n\n**Recovery**: Not recoverable; indicates poll loop is blocked too long.\n\n```java\ntry {\n    consumer.commitSync();\n} catch (CommitFailedException e) {\n    // Consumer lost group membership\n    // Exit poll loop and rejoin\n    break;\n}\n```\n\n### RetriableCommitFailedException\n\n**When**: Transient commit failure; can retry.\n\n**Causes**:\n- Broker temporarily unavailable\n- Network timeout\n- Rebalance in progress\n\n**Recovery**: Retry or wait for transient condition to pass.\n\n```java\ntry {\n    consumer.commitAsync(offsets, (offsets, ex) -> {\n        if (ex instanceof RetriableCommitFailedException) {\n            // Retry later\n        }\n    });\n} catch (RetriableCommitFailedException e) {\n    // Retry in next poll\n}\n```\n\n### OffsetOutOfRangeException\n\n**When**: Seeking to invalid offset (not in broker log).\n\n**Causes**:\n- Offset smaller than log start (old messages deleted)\n- Offset larger than log end\n- Partition doesn't exist\n\n**Recovery**: Use `auto.offset.reset` policy or explicitly seek to valid range.\n\n```java\ntry {\n    consumer.poll(Duration.ofSeconds(1));\n} catch (OffsetOutOfRangeException e) {\n    // Handle invalid offset\n    consumer.seekToBeginning(consumer.assignment());\n}\n```\n\n### NoOffsetForPartitionException\n\n**When**: No offset available for partition (never committed, offset expired).\n\n**Recovery**: Use `auto.offset.reset` to determine fallback behavior.\n\n### InvalidOffsetException\n\n**When**: Offset initialization fails; unrecoverable.\n\n**Indicates**: Configuration or state issue; usually fatal.\n\n### WakeupException\n\n**When**: Another thread called `wakeup()`.\n\n**Behavior**: Interrupts blocking operation (poll, commit, etc.).\n\n**Pattern**:\n\n```java\ntry {\n    consumer.poll(Duration.ofSeconds(1));\n} catch (WakeupException e) {\n    if (shutdownRequested) {\n        // Expected; exit gracefully\n        break;\n    } else {\n        // Unexpected; rethrow\n        throw e;\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### InterruptException\n\n**When**: Consumer thread was interrupted (via `Thread.interrupt()`).\n\n**Note**: `WakeupException` is preferred; `InterruptException` supported for compatibility.\n\n### AuthenticationException\n\n**When**: Authentication credentials invalid or expired.\n\n**Recoverable**: No; indicates configuration issue.\n\n### AuthorizationException\n\n**When**: Consumer lacks permissions for topics/group.\n\n**Recoverable**: No; requires permission changes.\n\n### RebalanceInProgressException\n\n**When**: Sync commit fails because rebalance in progress.\n\n**Recovery**: Retry after `poll()` completes rebalance.\n\n```java\nwhile (true) {\n    try {\n        consumer.commitSync();\n        break;\n    } catch (RebalanceInProgressException e) {\n        consumer.poll(Duration.ofSeconds(1));  // Complete rebalance\n        // Try commit again\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### FencedInstanceIdException\n\n**When**: Another consumer with same `group.instance.id` joined group.\n\n**Cause**: Two instances with same static member ID.\n\n**Recovery**: Ensure unique instance IDs or wait for fencing timeout.\n\n---\n\n## Configuration-Driven Behaviors\n\n### Offset Reset Policy (`auto.offset.reset`)\n\n**Applies When**: No committed offset found for partition.\n\n```properties\nauto.offset.reset=earliest    # Start from beginning\nauto.offset.reset=latest      # Start from end\nauto.offset.reset=none        # Throw NoOffsetForPartitionException\n```\n\n### Commit Behavior (`enable.auto.commit`, `auto.commit.interval.ms`)\n\n```properties\nenable.auto.commit=true       # Automatic commits (default)\nauto.commit.interval.ms=5000  # Every 5 seconds\n\nenable.auto.commit=false      # Manual commits only\n```\n\n### Poll Timeout and Batch Size\n\n```properties\nfetch.max.wait.ms=500       # Broker waits up to 500ms for batch\nfetch.min.bytes=1           # Minimum bytes to return\nmax.poll.records=500        # Max records per poll\n```\n\n### Heartbeat and Session\n\n```properties\nheartbeat.interval.ms=3000         # Send heartbeat every 3 seconds\nsession.timeout.ms=10000           # Die if no heartbeat for 10 seconds\nmax.poll.interval.ms=300000        # Die if no poll for 5 minutes\n```\n\n### Isolation Level\n\n```properties\nisolation.level=read_uncommitted   # Read all messages (default)\nisolation.level=read_committed     # Skip aborted transactions\n```\n\nWith `read_committed`:\n- `poll()` filters out aborted transaction messages\n- `seekToEnd()` seeks to LSO (Last Stable Offset)\n- `endOffsets()` returns LSO\n- Transactional messages have gaps in offsets\n\n---\n\n## Common Patterns and Best Practices\n\n### Pattern 1: Simple Group-Managed Consumer\n\n```java\nProperties props = new Properties();\nprops.setProperty(\"bootstrap.servers\", \"localhost:9092\");\nprops.setProperty(\"group.id\", \"my-group\");\nprops.setProperty(\"key.deserializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringDeserializer\");\nprops.setProperty(\"value.deserializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringDeserializer\");\nprops.setProperty(\"auto.offset.reset\", \"earliest\");\n\ntry (KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props)) {\n    consumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic\"));\n\n    while (true) {\n        ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n        for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n            System.out.printf(\"offset = %d, key = %s, value = %s%n\",\n                record.offset(), record.key(), record.value());\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### Pattern 2: Manual Offset Management\n\n```java\nprops.setProperty(\"enable.auto.commit\", \"false\");\n\ntry (KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props)) {\n    consumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic\"));\n\n    while (true) {\n        ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n\n        for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n            try {\n                processRecord(record);\n            } catch (Exception e) {\n                handleError(record, e);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Commit when batch is done\n        consumer.commitSync();\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### Pattern 3: Exactly-Once Semantics with External Store\n\n```java\nprops.setProperty(\"enable.auto.commit\", \"false\");\n\ntry (KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props)) {\n    consumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic\"), new ConsumerRebalanceListener() {\n        @Override\n        public void onPartitionsRevoked(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n            // Commit current state + offsets together\n            saveState();\n        }\n\n        @Override\n        public void onPartitionsAssigned(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n            // Restore state from external store\n            restoreState();\n        }\n    });\n\n    while (true) {\n        ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n\n        // Process in transaction with state update\n        try {\n            processRecordsInTransaction(records);\n            commitStateAndOffsets(records);\n        } catch (Exception e) {\n            rollbackState();\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### Pattern 4: Single Consumer Thread + Worker Pool\n\n```java\nint numWorkers = 8;\nBlockingQueue<ConsumerRecords<String, String>> queue = new LinkedBlockingQueue<>(100);\n\n// Consumer thread\nThread consumerThread = new Thread(() -> {\n    try (KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props)) {\n        consumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic\"));\n\n        while (!Thread.interrupted()) {\n            ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofSeconds(1));\n            if (!records.isEmpty()) {\n                queue.put(records);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n});\n\n// Worker threads\nExecutorService workers = Executors.newFixedThreadPool(numWorkers);\nfor (int i = 0; i < numWorkers; i++) {\n    workers.submit(() -> {\n        while (!Thread.interrupted()) {\n            try {\n                ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = queue.poll(1, TimeUnit.SECONDS);\n                if (records != null) {\n                    for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n                        processRecord(record);\n                    }\n                }\n            } catch (InterruptedException e) {\n                break;\n            }\n        }\n    });\n}\n\nconsumerThread.start();\n// ... later ...\nconsumerThread.interrupt();\nworkers.shutdown();\nworkers.awaitTermination(1, TimeUnit.MINUTES);\n```\n\n### Pattern 5: Pause/Resume for Flow Control\n\n```java\nMap<TopicPartition, Long> targetOffsets = new HashMap<>();\n\nconsumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic\"));\n\nwhile (true) {\n    ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n\n    // Check lag and pause fast partitions\n    for (TopicPartition partition : consumer.assignment()) {\n        long position = consumer.position(partition);\n        long lag = consumer.currentLag(partition).orElse(0);\n\n        if (lag > MAX_LAG) {\n            consumer.pause(Collections.singleton(partition));\n        } else {\n            consumer.resume(Collections.singleton(partition));\n        }\n    }\n\n    for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n        processRecord(record);\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### Pattern 6: Manual Partition Assignment for Stateful Processing\n\n```java\nString topic = \"events\";\n// Manually assign specific partitions\nTopicPartition partition0 = new TopicPartition(topic, 0);\nTopicPartition partition1 = new TopicPartition(topic, 1);\n\nconsumer.assign(Arrays.asList(partition0, partition1));\n\n// Restore position from local state store\nconsumer.seek(partition0, localStore.getOffset(partition0));\nconsumer.seek(partition1, localStore.getOffset(partition1));\n\nwhile (true) {\n    ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n\n    for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n        processRecord(record);\n        localStore.updateOffset(record.partition(), record.offset() + 1);\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### Pattern 7: Transactional Message Consumption\n\n```java\nprops.setProperty(\"isolation.level\", \"read_committed\");\n\ntry (KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props)) {\n    consumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic\"));\n\n    while (true) {\n        ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n\n        // Only committed transactional messages are returned\n        for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n            // Safe to process; definitely committed\n            processRecord(record);\n        }\n\n        consumer.commitSync();\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### Best Practices\n\n1. **Always close**: Use try-with-resources or finally block\n2. **One thread per consumer**: Never share between threads\n3. **Handle CommitFailedException**: Indicates need to rejoin group\n4. **Tune max.poll.interval.ms**: Based on expected processing time\n5. **Use committed offset semantics**: Commit = next offset to consume\n6. **Handle rebalances**: Implement ConsumerRebalanceListener properly\n7. **Avoid long processing**: Move to separate threads if needed\n8. **Monitor lag**: Use `currentLag()` or metrics\n9. **Test exception paths**: Simulate broker failures, network issues\n10. **Log poll loop latency**: Detect slow polls indicating problems\n\n---\n\n## Usage Examples\n\n### Example 1: Basic Subscription and Consumption\n\n```java\nProperties props = new Properties();\nprops.setProperty(\"bootstrap.servers\", \"localhost:9092\");\nprops.setProperty(\"group.id\", \"test-group\");\nprops.setProperty(\"enable.auto.commit\", \"true\");\nprops.setProperty(\"auto.commit.interval.ms\", \"1000\");\nprops.setProperty(\"key.deserializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringDeserializer\");\nprops.setProperty(\"value.deserializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringDeserializer\");\n\nKafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props);\nconsumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic1\", \"topic2\"));\n\ntry {\n    while (true) {\n        ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n        for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n            System.out.printf(\"topic=%s, partition=%d, offset=%d, key=%s, value=%s%n\",\n                record.topic(), record.partition(), record.offset(),\n                record.key(), record.value());\n        }\n    }\n} finally {\n    consumer.close();\n}\n```\n\n### Example 2: Rebalance Listener with Manual Commits\n\n```java\nProperties props = new Properties();\nprops.setProperty(\"bootstrap.servers\", \"localhost:9092\");\nprops.setProperty(\"group.id\", \"test-group\");\nprops.setProperty(\"enable.auto.commit\", \"false\");\nprops.setProperty(\"key.deserializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringDeserializer\");\nprops.setProperty(\"value.deserializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringDeserializer\");\n\nKafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props);\n\nConsumerRebalanceListener listener = new ConsumerRebalanceListener() {\n    @Override\n    public void onPartitionsRevoked(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n        System.out.println(\"Committing offsets for revoked partitions: \" + partitions);\n        consumer.commitSync();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void onPartitionsAssigned(Collection<TopicPartition> partitions) {\n        System.out.println(\"New partitions assigned: \" + partitions);\n    }\n};\n\nconsumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic\"), listener);\n\ntry {\n    while (true) {\n        ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n        for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n            System.out.printf(\"offset=%d, key=%s, value=%s%n\",\n                record.offset(), record.key(), record.value());\n        }\n\n        // Commit offsets after processing batch\n        consumer.commitSync();\n    }\n} finally {\n    consumer.close();\n}\n```\n\n### Example 3: Seek to Timestamp\n\n```java\nProperties props = new Properties();\nprops.setProperty(\"bootstrap.servers\", \"localhost:9092\");\nprops.setProperty(\"group.id\", \"test-group\");\nprops.setProperty(\"key.deserializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringDeserializer\");\nprops.setProperty(\"value.deserializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringDeserializer\");\n\nKafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props);\nconsumer.assign(Arrays.asList(\n    new TopicPartition(\"topic\", 0),\n    new TopicPartition(\"topic\", 1)\n));\n\n// Seek to messages from 1 hour ago\nlong oneHourAgo = System.currentTimeMillis() - (60 * 60 * 1000);\nMap<TopicPartition, Long> timestamps = new HashMap<>();\nfor (TopicPartition partition : consumer.assignment()) {\n    timestamps.put(partition, oneHourAgo);\n}\n\nMap<TopicPartition, OffsetAndTimestamp> offsets = consumer.offsetsForTimes(timestamps);\nfor (Map.Entry<TopicPartition, OffsetAndTimestamp> entry : offsets.entrySet()) {\n    if (entry.getValue() != null) {\n        consumer.seek(entry.getKey(), entry.getValue().offset());\n    }\n}\n\ntry {\n    while (true) {\n        ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n        for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n            System.out.printf(\"timestamp=%d, offset=%d, value=%s%n\",\n                record.timestamp(), record.offset(), record.value());\n        }\n    }\n} finally {\n    consumer.close();\n}\n```\n\n### Example 4: Multi-Threaded Processing with Pause/Resume\n\n```java\nBlockingQueue<ConsumerRecord<String, String>> queue = new LinkedBlockingQueue<>(1000);\nboolean shutdown = false;\n\n// Consumer thread\nThread consumerThread = new Thread(() -> {\n    Properties props = new Properties();\n    props.setProperty(\"bootstrap.servers\", \"localhost:9092\");\n    props.setProperty(\"group.id\", \"test-group\");\n    props.setProperty(\"key.deserializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringDeserializer\");\n    props.setProperty(\"value.deserializer\", \"org.apache.kafka.common.serialization.StringDeserializer\");\n\n    KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props);\n    consumer.subscribe(Arrays.asList(\"topic\"));\n\n    try {\n        while (!shutdown) {\n            ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofMillis(100));\n            for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n                queue.put(record);\n\n                // Pause if queue is getting full\n                if (queue.size() > 800) {\n                    consumer.pause(consumer.assignment());\n                } else if (queue.size() < 200) {\n                    consumer.resume(consumer.assignment());\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    } finally {\n        consumer.close();\n    }\n});\n\n// Worker thread\nThread workerThread = new Thread(() -> {\n    while (!shutdown) {\n        try {\n            ConsumerRecord<String, String> record = queue.poll(1, TimeUnit.SECONDS);\n            if (record != null) {\n                processRecord(record);\n            }\n        } catch (InterruptedException e) {\n            Thread.currentThread().interrupt();\n        }\n    }\n});\n\nconsumerThread.start();\nworkerThread.start();\n\n// Later, shutdown\nshutdown = true;\nconsumerThread.join();\nworkerThread.join();\n```\n\n---\n\n## Conclusion\n\nThe Kafka `KafkaConsumer` API provides powerful abstractions for reliable, scalable message consumption. Success with the consumer depends on understanding:\n\n1. **Threading model**: Single-threaded, with `wakeup()` for cross-thread interruption\n2. **Offset semantics**: Committed offset = next offset to consume\n3. **Group coordination**: Automatic partition assignment with rebalance callbacks\n4. **Poll semantics**: May block longer than timeout, runs rebalance callbacks\n5. **Position control**: Fine-grained control over consumption position\n6. **Error handling**: CommitFailedException indicates lost membership\n\nBy combining these building blocks with the patterns shown, you can build robust Kafka consumers for almost any consumption use case.\n",

## Overview

The `KafkaConsumer<K, V>` is a Java client for consuming records from Apache Kafka clusters. It provides a flexible API supporting multiple consumption patterns:

- **Group-managed consumption**: Multiple consumer instances automatically partition work through group coordination
- **Standalone consumption**: Manual partition assignment for independent consumers
- **Dynamic topic subscription**: Subscribe to topics and automatically discover new partitions
- **Manual offset management**: Either automatic or explicit offset commits

### Key Characteristics

- **Not thread-safe**: The consumer instance itself must be confined to a single thread. Only `wakeup()` is thread-safe.
- **Event loop model**: The consumer processes rebalances and manages group membership only during `poll()` calls
- **Transparent broker failure handling**: Automatically reconnects to available brokers
